249→func buildNotifierConfig(alertmanagers []ExternalAMcfg) (*config.Config, map[string]http.Header, error) {\n   250→\tamConfigs := make([]*config.AlertmanagerConfig, 0, len(alertmanagers))\n   251→\theaders := map[string]http.Header{}\n   252→\tfor i, am := range alertmanagers {\n   253→\t\tu, err := url.Parse(am.URL)\n   254→\t\tif err != nil {\n   255→\t\t\treturn nil, nil, err\n 274→\t\t\tPathPrefix:              u.Path,\n   275→\t\t\tTimeout:                 model.Duration(timeout),\n   276→\t\t\tServiceDiscoveryConfigs: sdConfig,\n   277→\t\t}\n   278→\n   279→\t\tif 287→\t\t\tamConfig.HTTPClientConfig.BasicAuth = &common_config.BasicAuth{\n   288→\t\t\t\tUsername: u.User.Username(),\n   289→\t\t\t}\n   290→\n   291→\t\t\tif password, isSet := u.User.Password(); 297→\n   298→\tnotifierConfig := &config.Config{\n   299→\t\tAlertingConfig: config.AlertingConfig{\n   300→\t\t\tAlertmanagerConfigs: amConfigs,\n   301→\t\t},\n   302→\t}\n   303→\n   304→\treturn for annotations/labels than grafana's internal alertmanager, so we sanitize invalid keys.\n   309→\treturn &Alert{\n   310→\t\tLabels:       s.options.sanitizeLabelSetFn(alert.Labels),\n   311→\t\tAnnotations:  s.options.sanitizeLabelSetFn(alert.Annotations),\n   312→\t\tStartsAt:     time.Time(alert.StartsAt),\n   313→\t\tEndsAt:       time.Time(alert.EndsAt),\n   314→\t\tGeneratorURL: alert.GeneratorURL.String(),\n   315→\t}\n   316→}\n   317→\n   318→// sanitizeLabelSet sanitizes all given LabelSet keys according to sanitizeLabelName.\n   319→// If there is a collision as a result of sanitization, a short (6 char) md5 hash of the original key will be added as a suffix.\n   320→func (s *ExternalAlertmanager) sanitizeLabelSet(lbls models.LabelSet) labels.Labels {\n   321→\tls := make(labels.Labels, 0, len(lbls))\n   322→\tset := make(map[string]struct{})\n   323→\n   324→\t// Must sanitize labels in order otherwise resulting label set can be inconsistent when there are collisions.\n   325→\tfor _, k := range sortedKeys(lbls) {\n   326→\t\tsanitizedLabelName, err := s.sanitizeLabelName(k)\n   327→\t\tif err != nil {\n   328→\t\t\ts.logger.Error(\"Alert sending to external Alertmanager(s) contains an invalid label/annotation name that failed to sanitize, skipping\", \"name\", k, \"error\", err)\n   329→\t\t\tcontinue\n   330→\t\t}\n   331→\n   332→\t\t// There can be label name collisions after we sanitize. We check for this and attempt to make the name unique again using a short hash of the original name.\n   333→\t\tif _, ok := set[sanitizedLabelName]; ok {\n   334→\t\t\tsanitizedLabelName = sanitizedLabelName + fmt.Sprintf(\"_%.3x\", md5.Sum([]byte(k)))\n   335→\t\t\ts.logger.Warn(\"Alert contains duplicate label/annotation name after sanitization, appending unique suffix\", \"name\", k, \"newName\", sanitizedLabelName, \"error\", err)\n   336→\t\t}\n   337→\n   338→\t\tset[sanitizedLabelName] = struct{}{}\n   339→\t\tls = append(ls, labels.Label{Name: sanitizedLabelName, Value: lbls[k]})\n   340→\t}\n   341→\n   342→\treturn ls\n   343→}\n   344→\n   345→// sanitizeLabelName will fix a given label name so that it is compatible with prometheus alertmanager character restrictions.\n   346→// Prometheus alertmanager requires labels to match ^[a-zA-Z_][a-zA-Z0-9_]*$.\n   347→// Characters with an ASCII code < 127 will be replaced with an underscore (_), characters with ASCII code >= 127 will be replaced by their hex representation.\n   348→// For backwards compatibility, whitespace will be removed instead of replaced with an underscore.\n   349→func (s *ExternalAlertmanager) sanitizeLabelName(name string) (string, error) {\n   350→\tif len(name) == 0 {\n   351→\t\treturn \"\", errors.New(\"label name cannot be empty\")\n   352→\t}\n   353→\n   354→\tif isValidLabelName(name) {\n   355→\t\treturn name, nil\n   356→\t}\n   357→\n   358→\ts.logger.Warn(\"Alert sending to external Alertmanager(s) contains label/annotation name with invalid characters\", \"name\", name)\n   359→\n   360→\t// Remove spaces. We do this instead of replacing with underscore for backwards compatibility as this existed before the rest of this function.\n   361→\tsanitized := strings.Join(strings.Fields(name), \"\")\n   362→\n   363→\t// Replace other invalid characters.\n   364→\tvar buf strings.Builder\n   365→\tfor i, b := range sanitized {\n   366→\t\tif isValidCharacter(i, b) {\n   367→\t\t\tbuf.WriteRune(b)\n   368→\t\t\tcontinue\n   369→\t\t}\n   370→\n   371→\t\tif b <= unicode.MaxASCII {\n   372→\t\t\tbuf.WriteRune('_')\n   373→\t\t\tcontinue\n   374→\t\t}\n   375→\n   376→\t\tif i == 0 {\n   377→\t\t\tbuf.WriteRune('_')\n   378→\t\t}\n   379→\t\t_, _ = fmt.Fprintf(&buf, \"%#x\", b)\n   380→\t}\n   381→\n   382→\tif buf.Len() == 0 {\n   383→\t\treturn \"\", fmt.Errorf(\"label name is empty after removing invalids chars\")\n   384→\t}\n   385→\n   386→\treturn buf.String(), nil\n   387→}\n   388→\n   389→// isValidLabelName is true iff the label name matches the pattern of ^[a-zA-Z_][a-zA-Z0-9_]*$.\n   390→func isValidLabelName(ln string) bool {\n   391→\tif len(ln) == 0 {\n   392→\t\treturn false\n   393→\t}\n   394→\tfor i, b := range ln {\n   395→\t\tif !isValidCharacter(i, b) {\n   396→\t\t\treturn false\n   397→\t\t}\n   398→\t}\n   399→\treturn true\n   400→}\n   401→\n   402→// isValidCharacter checks if a specific rune is allowed at the given position in a label key for an external Prometheus alertmanager.\n   403→// From alertmanager LabelName.IsValid().\n   404→func isValidCharacter(pos int, b rune) bool {\n   405→\treturn (b >= 'a' && b <= 'z') || (b >= 'A' && b <= 'Z') || b == '_' || (b >= '0' && b <= '9' && pos > 0)\n   406→}\n   407→\n   408→func sortedKeys(m map[string]string) []string {\n   409→\torderedKeys := make([]string, len(m))\n   410→\ti := 0\n   411→\tfor k := range m {\n   412→\t\torderedKeys[i] = k\n   413→\t\ti++\n   414→\t}\n   415→\tsort.Strings(orderedKeys)\n   416→\treturn orderedKeys\n   417→}\n sanitizeLabelName.\n// If there is a collision as a result of sanitization, a short (6 char) md5 hash of the original key will be added as a suffix.\nfunc (s *ExternalAlertmanager) sanitizeLabelSet(lbls models.LabelSet) labels.Labels {\n\tls := make(labels.Labels, 0, len(lbls))\n\tset := make(map[string]struct{})\n\n\t// Must sanitize labels in order otherwise resulting label collisions after we sanitize. `pkg/services/ngalert/schedule/schedule.go:Run()`, which initiates the `schedulePeriodic()` loop that ticks at regular intervals. On each tick, `processTick()` determines which alert rules should be evaluated based on their evaluation interval.\\n\\n## Rule Evaluation\\nFor each scheduled rule, the alert rule's `Eval()` method in `pkg/services/ngalert/schedule/alert_rule.go` is called. This triggers the `evaluate()` method which:\\n1. Creates an evaluator from the `eval.EvaluatorFactory` (defined in `pkg/services/ngalert/eval/eval.go`)\\n2. Calls the `ConditionEvaluator.Evaluate()` method to execute the alert condition against datasources\\n3. Returns evaluation results containing alert instance data\\n\\n## State Transition Management\\nEvaluation results are passed to the State Manager's `ProcessEvalResults()` method in `pkg/services/ngalert/state/manager.go`. This:\\n1. Calls `setNextStateForRule()` which processes each evaluation result\\n2. For each result, calls the `State.transition()` method in `pkg/services/ngalert/state/state.go` to determine state changes\\n3. Records whether each alert instance transitioned (e.g., Normal → Alerting, Alerting → Normal)\\n4. Generates `StateTransition` objects describing what changed\\n5. Invokes the optional `Sender` callback to dispatch notifications\\n\\n## Alert Notification Dispatch\\nThe `send()` method in `pkg/services/ngalert/schedule/alert_rule.go` converts state transitions to `PostableAlerts` and calls the `AlertsSender.Send()` method. This is implemented by the `AlertsRouter` in `pkg/services/ngalert/sender/router.go`.\\n\\n`AlertsRouter.Send()` determines routing based on organization configuration:\\n- For **internal notifications**: Calls `MultiOrgAlertmanager.AlertmanagerFor()` in `pkg/services/ngalert/notifier/multiorg_alertmanager.go` to get the org's alertmanager, then calls `PutAlerts()` on the underlying `alertmanager` struct in `pkg/services/ngalert/notifier/alertmanager.go`\\n- For **external notifications**: Calls `ExternalAlertmanager.SendAlerts()` in `pkg/services/ngalert/sender/sender.go` which sends alerts to configured external Alertmanager(s)\\n\\nThe internal alertmanager processes alerts through the notification routing tree based on receiver configuration, while external alertmanagers receive alerts via their API endpoints for further routing and notification delivery to receivers (email, Slack, PagerDuty, etc.).\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
